houses, in july 2016, tanihub started to become a business to business suppliers for all agriculture commodities – fruit, vegetable, poultry, fishery, livestock. with the support of tanixpress, delivering agriculture products from farms to market with affordable price, efficient sourcing, and reliable supply chain. the aim is to bring forward indonesia by giving market access to as many dimana financial advisor bertugas untuk merencanakan, dan memasarkan produk asuransi sesuai dengan kebutuhan nasabah sedangkan service dimana fa juga berperan dalam pelayanan klaim ataupun komplain
